As we approach the mid of the month, it’s pathetic and disappointing to see that both New Customer Acquisition (NCA) and Investments continue to perform below expectations across all regions.

We started this month with clear targets, action plans, and the potential to convert leads into lasting relationships. Yet, somewhere between daily routines and distractions, the momentum seems to have dipped.

We need to ask ourselves:
* Have we become too complacent after initial efforts?
* Are we treating DRR as optional?
* Are field activities and customer interactions being done with seriousness?

We cannot afford to lose ground in a highly competitive market. If we don’t stay aggressive and proactive now, recovery at month-end will be impossible.

What Needs to Happen Immediately:
🔸 Area heads must conduct daily reviews with concerned branch team
🔸 All pending investment leads must be closed/followed up with urgency
🔸 Each team member must bring in at least one new customer per day this week
🔸 Investment and NCA performance to be tracked daily at the HO level

Let’s be very clear:
This is not a routine month. Expectations are high, and delivery is non-negotiable. We need visible action, aggressive fieldwork, and real conversions.

The second half of the month must show a complete turnaround, and Management will directly be reviewing low performing region’s by the 17th.

Regards,
Abin James

09/06/25, 9:13 pm - Abin Sir RCIL: T&C:

1. Customer Composition: Each branch conducting a customer meet must ensure a 70:30 ratio (70% new customers & 30% existing customers) if it is a branch already conducted a meet.

2. Customer List Approval: The customer list must be verified and approved by the concerned Area Manager (AM) before being submitted to the Head Office (H.O).

3. Minimum Participation: A minimum of 150 investors must be present at each Investors Meet.

4. Data Accuracy: All customer details submitted (name, contact, investment) must be accurate, updated, and verifiable. Format will be shared soon.

5. Branch Collaboration: Branches may collaborate to conduct joint events, provided they meet the overall customer target and maintain quality engagement. (Collalaborated branches should have a minimum of 200 investors) 

6. Venue Standards: Venues should be easily accessible, with proper seating and audio-visual setup

7. Staff Participation: Branch Managers and designated  branch team must be present throughout the event to support customer interaction and make the meet a success.

Please note that now onwards “Attendance Regularization” option in HRMS has been switched to “Punching Regularization.”

Use the Punching Regularization option in HRMS to regularize your attendance.

Important Guidelines:

For punching regularization, railway time format (24-hour format) must be used (e.g., to regularize 5:30 PM, select 17:30 from the time selection). Manual time entry is not allowed.

Punching regularization requests must be submitted in HRMS within 48 hours. After this period, the dates will be locked and further requests will not be accepted.


For your reference, a demo video on how to apply Punching Regularization has been attached. Please watch it before submitting your request.

For any queries or clarifications, please contact the HR department via email.

We're writing to provide a detailed update on the Appraisal and profit-sharing process for the financial year 2024-25. We know how important this is to each of you, and we appreciate your continued hard work and dedication throughout the year.

The appraisal process is progressing well, and we're currently in the final stages of completing the profit-sharing calculations. This involves careful review and validation to ensure accuracy and fairness for all eligible employees. Due to the comprehensive nature of this work, there will be a slight delay in the disbursement of both your increment and profit-sharing amounts.

We understand that you're eager to know the outcome, and we want to assure you that this entire process will be completed shortly. You will receive formal communication detailing your individual appraisal outcome, including your revised salary and profit-sharing eligibility, by August 16, 2025. This letter will be sent directly to your personal email address.

Here’s a clear breakdown of when you can expect these amounts to be disbursed:

Profit-sharing amounts for all eligible staff members will be disbursed along with your monthly salary from August 2025 onwards.

Your revised salary, reflecting any applicable increments and including any arrears from the effective date, will also be credited to your account along with your salary for the month of August 2025.

We genuinely appreciate your patience and understanding as we finalize these important details. Our goal is to ensure that everything is processed accurately and efficiently.

Thank you for your continued contributions.

Best regards,

Titto Joseph

23/08/25, 5:46 pm - Hr Reliant: Sub: *Revised Attendance & Leave Management Policy (RCIL/HRD-005)*

The Management has decided to revise the Attendance & Leave Management Policy (Policy Code: RCIL/HRD-005) with respect to late coming and early leaving. A grace period of 15 minutes will be allowed either for coming/going after or before the stipulated time instead of 45 minutes. This change will take effect from August 26, 2025. 

Late or Early mark rules: 

5 times in a month, every employee is allowed a 15-minute grace time for coming/going after or before the stipulated time. Any employee coming late / going early after or before the grace period of 15 minutes for more than 5 times in a month will be marked half day for the said day. The same should be either deducted from his/her leave balance, or in the absence of sufficient leave balance, salary in lieu of leave will be deducted. 


With Regards, 

HR Department 
Reliant Credits (India) Ltd.

04/09/25, 8:44 pm - Abin Sir RCIL: Dear All,

Please find below the steps to onboard a new investor for the NCD (Non-Convertible Debenture) P Series:

Onboarding a New NCD Holder:
1. Duly filled and signed Debenture Application P-Seriea and Part-B of the NCD Application Form
2. Copy of PAN Card and Aadhar Card
3. Demat Account – Client Master Details

Note: If the customer does not have a Demat Account, please follow the "Steps to Open a Demat Account" outlined below.

Please find the attached “Debenture Application Form.”
Important: All fields in the application form must be completed.

Steps to Open a Demat Account:
1. Copy of PAN Card
2. Copy of Aadhar Card
3. Bank Proof (either a cancelled cheque with printed name, or the first and latest transaction page of the bank passbook)
4. Signature on a plain white sheet (for scanning)
5. Recent passport-size photograph
6. Mother’s Name
7. Email ID
8. Mobile Number (must be Aadhar-linked)

For any queries related to Demat account opening, please contact the Investment Department.


Regards,
